  <script type="text/javascript">
   function TI_createCookie(name,value,days,cookieDomain) {
        var expires = "";

        if (!cookieDomain) {
            cookieDomain = "";
        }

        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
            expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
        }
        document.cookie = name+"="+value+";domain="+cookieDomain+"; path=/"+expires;
    }

    function TI_readCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }

    function TI_eraseCookie(name) {
        createCookie(name,"",-1);
    }

    function getAllElementsWithAttribute(attribute)
    {
        var matchingElements = [];
        var allElements = document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        for (var i = 0, n = allElements.length; i < n; i++)
        {
            if (allElements[i].getAttribute(attribute) !== null)
            {
                // Element exists with attribute. Add to array.
                matchingElements.push(allElements[i]);
            }
        }
        return matchingElements;
    }

    function addEvent(element, method) {
        if (element.addEventListener) {
            element.addEventListener("click", method, false);
        }
        else {
            element.attachEvent("onclick", method);
        }
    }

    async function setOMDContact() {
        try {

            var trackingId = _stTracker.getUserIdentifier();

            if (trackingId != null) {

                Http = new XMLHttpRequest();

                url = "/api/ui/trackingapi/registertracking?id=" + trackingId + "";
                Http.open("POST", url);
                Http.send();

                Http.onreadystatechange = (e) => {
                    console.log(Http.responseText)
                }
            }
        }
        catch (error) {
            console.log(error);
        }
    }

           <div class="navigation-dropdown__tout spacer-sm">
            <h2 class="navigation-dropdown__title">
             Getting here
            </h2>
            <div class="navigation-dropdown__subtitle">
             With so many air routes to choose from, Ireland is accessible no matter where you are in the world.
